## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Characters\5 Stages Of Grief.md

A cyborg with 5 exo skeletons that add to the body. Only Combined they are like a gundam the are grief.

5 songs is all we need.
5 interlockable body parts

Mulholland Drive's 5 Stages of Grief as shown through its characters: 

Denial - Rita 
When something terrible happens, the world suddenly appears meaningless and overwhelming. So we may cling to a false, preferable reality, and avoid any reminders of the truth. When we hear that a loved one died, we might hold on to hope that maybe they just identified the wrong person, or through some unlikely event, our loved one actually made it out okay. 

Anger - Adam 
When we can no longer deny our situation, we may become enraged, as if something incredibly unfair has just happened to us weâ€™re left to wonder what we did to deserve it.Â Anger is, in a way, a kind of strength that can give the illusion of structure to the hollowness of loss. 

Bargaining - Betty 
Hoping we can avoid grief, a period of bargaining may occur, taking the form of an emotional truce. All of our â€œWhat ifsâ€ and â€œIf onlysâ€ remind us of our faults and what we could have done differently. A negotiation for a better outcome is often made in exchange for a reformed lifestyle. We might try and create a better version of ourselves, worthy of a happier ending. 

Depression - Diane 
Eventually, our attention circles back to the here and now. Finally recognizing our situation, we may fall into despair. We become silent, reclusive and spend most of our time in a fog of intense sadness. 

Acceptance - Cowboy 
In this final stage, we embrace the inevitable future, or tragic event. We accept that our loved one is physically gone and recognize that this new reality is permanent. We are able, in some way, to move on. Of course in this filmâ€¦ well, this last part doesnâ€™t really happenâ€¦ â€œNot Acceptanceâ€ - The Bum

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Characters\The Cloud.md

The cloud has an ability to appear and formulate at any given point and place. It is fulled from the two fundamental elements water and information. When in the shape of a server farm it is bound to binary logic, semantics, and poetry, when in the form of vapour it linked directly to the physics, emotions and senses.
Itâ€™s purpose is ever changing. It functions as a messenger, keeper, and fuel for organic life.

In the story the clouds passive and being interpreted into. Itâ€™s an illusionary utopian all knowing projection of the protagonists desire to hold together more than their physical body and mind are capable.

The cloud is unpredictable, gets angry and spits out, instead of giving answers to those merging it gives them merely a greater understanding of their insignificance and limitations of their bodies minds. 

The vapourized form is like a happy sheep in a Heide movie. The digital is a bondage fanatic and into constraints and self torture but both offer tranquility to those entering them. The effective loathing effects are open for debate.

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Goals - Strategy.md

The aim is to fit the pope character into a non-linear story telling via social media to gain popularity to allow for concerts.  But also use the vertical Format as the stage.

### Plot ideas
realisations story, in which the pope tries something and ends up more confused or unhappy about the results of their efforts in the end.
A virtual sysiphos story giving comfort as  pope continuous to get up in the next video/episode.

### Performance
Movement's are hyper technical, NPC extreme, a dance, movement artform guided by technology.
### Visual 
Blend of generated and original content.
Mood according to scene
### Sound
comforting musical themes open each clip, and are nuanced counteracted, 
examples
angelic drones vs. deconstructed glitch beats
wobbely subs vs. high frequent thrills

# Noises to avoid
Turn of side projects that don't directly support the above mentioned goals if they don't pay money.
Vienna Struggle Radio Show 
Do not engage in Social Media at all until the above strategy is in place for roll out.
Limit to single social media platform.
do not go off brand, dedicated channel. do not use mandy mozart channel, or rebrand (ask expert)
# Length of campaigns

talk to experts (toxische pommes via anna, stefanie sargnagel direct)

assumption
4 Week cohorts with 1-4 posts a day (approximately 60 posts a month)
Adjust Posting Strategy (tags)

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Graphic Novel\About - Pocket Preacher.md

IMPORTANT REMARK ON WRITING STYLE...ENGAGE THE READER. ASK THEM TO SING THE SONG, ask them again. Ask them to sing out lout when a sing bubble pops up. Engage. like a kinder theater show. Puppentheater. make them yell and scream at the character, the phone. make them pet their phone when there is contemplation. make them turn off the phone proactively. make them spot to read and give them a time for reconnecting and reflecting. to ferment the thoughts

So, nun steigen wir auch schon einmal ein in dieses Mini Universum, dass da in deiner Hosentasche wartet entdeckt zu werden. 

Wir fangen an mit einer Pabst-Ã¤hnlichen Figur, die in einer ein bisschen in einer in der Zeit stehen gebliebene zu seinen Stadt jeden Tag einer ihr Gottgebenen TÃ¤tigkeit nachgeht. Fest im Glauben, souverÃ¤n in ihrer AusfÃ¼hrung, geschult in der Theologie, der Physik, der Mathematik, ja, all der Chemien, die ihre Welt zusammen halten. Anders als bei anderen Geschichten, scheint es kein Ã¤uÃŸerlich sichtbare Bedrohungen zu geben, es ist ein Leben, dass unsere Figur erlebt, der Routinen, der unerschÃ¼tterlichen Manifeste, der Rituale und einer gÃ¶ttlichen Ordnung. Es ist eine Stimme, die RealitÃ¤t schafft, und darin ist sich unsere Figur sicher, kann sie besonders gut. Ja, es gibt  nie"man"den auf Erden, die es besser kann...

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Graphic Novel\Cat Pope\Season 1 - Index.md

## Logline 
Cat Pope wird von einem mysteriÃ¶sen DoppelgÃ¤nger heimgesucht und begibt sich auf eine surreale Pilgerreise, auf der er sich GÃ¶ttern, Hexen und seinen tiefsten Ã„ngsten stellt. Unterwegs entdeckt er eine verblÃ¼ffende Wahrheit: Er und die seltsame Katze sind eins und zwingen ihn, seine wahre Natur zu erkennen und zu akzeptieren.

## Um was geht es in Cat Pope
Durch die dystopische Dekonstruktion einer der ikonichsten patriarchalen Figuren der Welt erzÃ¤hlt unsere Geschichte in Form einer modernen Fabel, wie einfach es sein kann die eigene SpiritualitÃ¤t und einen Platz in diesem Universum zu finden.

## Scope

5 Characters
11 Places

## Characters
### CAT 
A sphynx cat, the cat shaped version of the pope-like figure. The cat is mute and comments by observing and staring. Following the pope-like figure everywhere, and sort of enigmatically commenting on their behavior. 

### POPE-LIKE FIGURE 
A human preacher, believes to be heaven sent. A guide with huge responsibility, a strict discipline to ritual and magnificent fashion sense. They tend to monologue with rage and passion, internally and to anyone they meet.
[[Projects/Pocket Preacher/Characters/Cat Pope]]
### CAT POPE
The merged entity of cat and pope-like figure. Beliefs to be able to hide their true cat nature by acting.
### CHOIR
Is a mirror of the pope-like figures main repeating sermons and topics. They know all stories and plots ahead of time (because pope-like figure repeats everything all the time, nothing new ever comes from them). The choir appears in a angel like version from above, outside the frame and a manifested one, in appropriate situations. They are like the pope-like figures personal jukebox and commentary.

### KrÃ¤henwesen
[[KrÃ¤henwesen]]

In einem Kloster in den Berge hofft {PLF} schlieÃŸlich, Antworten auf die Verbindung zwischen ihr und der Katze zu finden. Die Bibliothek kommt zu keinem Ergebnis. Nach der Entdeckung eines geheimen Serverraums und besorgnisergenden Sourcecodes unter der Klosterbibliothek wird {PLF} erneut von KrÃ¤henwesen attackiert. Bereits beinahe dem Wahnsinn nah bricht ein Kampf aus und nur mit Einsatz einer Superkraft gelingt {PLF} die Flucht in den Friedhof des Klosters.

## EXT. ZWISCHEN DEN APARTMENTBLOCKS - BLAU STUNDE

Kathedralen-artige ragten die grauen Beton-Riesen bis hoch in den Himmel. Vom Regen glÃ¤nzten die Gehwege. Ein monotoner Drone-Chor erklang.

{PLF} flanierte durch die Gegend. {PLF} schien nicht in Eile zu sein und nahm hier und da Umwege. Es folgte eine Abfolge von Szenen, wie das Erkunden in einem MMORPG. Jede Szene war ein Schauplatz, in den {PLF} eintrat. Kurz dachte. Sich umsah. Kommentierte. Oft aber einfach Freude daran hatte zu verweilen.

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Graphic Novel\Season Ideas\School of Saints.md

A coming of age story about the formative years.

Cat pope and other spiritual figures in their adolescent years visit a high school that teaches them about the basics of spirituality and prepare them for saving the population of the world.

Taking place in a high school its a story about allies, friendships, love and hate, exploring sexuality, and social divide. 

Students and teachers are segregated in rich and poor faiths in which a main character has to over come many a more obstacles and temptations on their path to graduation.

The school teaches foremost how to become a saint, but not calling oneself one. The characters are driven by the urge to change the underlying system, but realize, that not only social status but prejeduice and social norm define, what is acceptable and how ones image is defined by action, not question.

"I give food to the poor, and they call me a saint. I ask why the poor have no food, and they call me a Communist." - Helder Camara (https://books.google.at/books?id=f7MJvhxmr4kC&pg=PA359&lpg=PA359&dq=%22I+give+food+to+the+poor,+and+they+call+me+a+saint.+I+ask+why+the+poor+have+no+food,+and+they+call+me+a+Communist.%22+-+Helder+Camara&source=bl&ots=YKR2r6g2er&sig=ACfU3U3KsUfpOKMvPz0YAaXsyMddEATWsw&hl=en&sa=X&ved=2ahUKEwjd8JLu6ZmEAxWeQ_EDHWm1D6MQ6AF6BAgdEAM#v=onepage&q=%22I%20give%20food%20to%20the%20poor%2C%20and%20they%20call%20me%20a%20saint.%20I%20ask%20why%20the%20poor%20have%20no%20food%2C%20and%20they%20call%20me%20a%20Communist.%22%20-%20Helder%20Camara&f=false)

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Project Outline.md

Preaching To The Choir

Telling people what they already know!
Affirming our selves!
Talking To The Magic Mirror!

A question of self realisation. What is the self, and what are the mechanism that even though we have more and more tools to look at our selves, it is harder and harder to feel okay with what we are.

Not just man have externalized their reputation. 

We, us, that's the choir! It's a dialog with our externalisations. They mirror is the first thing when it comes to explaining consciousness. An animal that recognizes itself, we call intelligent. 

Currently we are in the absurd assumption that NPCs are beings, people even tend to feel that way.

Looking at how we have perfected narcissim and self oberservation and even in a mirror like format (portrait vertical video is taking over) a new narrative is spinning. 

We are not seeing the stories of apostels and warriors and heros played out. we are constantly gazing at our selves, or people that look just like us, filtered by algorythms. 

I take this as a creative opportunity to develop characters and stories through movement, poetry, interaction, augumentation and sound. 

My work is multi facettet, can be viewed online, on screens and projections and in engaging live shows. 

But, Mirroring Excersices are also the fundation of syncing with the other in performance, how we learn. we carefully copy and follow. It's a sign of trust.

I am an optimist, and consider our current state of consciousness, that of collective first contact with ourselves on a different level. We have baked behavior sort of intuitively into our devices, now we are amazed that they behave like us, and belief them to be alive!

It's a fun time!

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Research\The Power of FATGA.md

Brilliant comparison by devisive historian 
[Niall Ferguson](https://www.spectator.co.uk/writer/niall-ferguson/) of the impact of big tech in terms of controlling the public space. In the end that what it comes down to with the preacher, who preaches the loudest, can they control the media that carries the message, and they will be heard. This is absolute rain. No need to bother with worldly matters, if one controls the CLOUD.
# Key Passages

"By the network platforms, I mean Facebook, Amazon, Twitter, Google and Apple, or FATGA for short â€” **companies that have established a dominance over the public sphere not seen since the heyday of the pre-Reformation Catholic Church.** FATGA had humble enough origins in garages and dorm rooms. As recently as 2008, not one of them could be found among the worldâ€™s largest companies by market capitalisation. Today, they occupy first, third, fourth and fifth places in the market cap league table, just above their Chinese counterparts, Tencent and Alibaba."

https://www.spectator.co.uk/article/the-tech-supremacy-silicon-valley-can-no-longer-conceal-its-power/

> 1. No provider or user of an interactive computer service shall be treated as the publisher or speaker of any information provided by another information content provider.2. No provider or user of an interactive computer service shall be held liable on account of â€¦ any action voluntarily taken in good faith to restrict access to or availability of material that the provider or user considers to be obscene, lewd, lascivious, filthy, excessively violent, harassing, or otherwise objectionable.

In essence, Section 230 gives websites immunity from liability for what their users post if it is in any way harmful, but also entitles websites to take down with equal impunity any content that they donâ€™t like the look of. The surely unintended result of this legislation, drafted for a fledgling internet, is that some of the biggest companies in the world enjoy a protection reminiscent of Joseph Hellerâ€™s _Catch-22_. Try to hold them responsible as publishers, and they will say they are platforms. Demand access to their platforms and they will insist that they are publishers.

## COMMENT
... spaeter im Text vergleicht er doch nicht so ganz unbiased Trump Riots (offensichtlich von ihm angestachelt mit dem wiederholen des STOLE THE ELECTION maerchen) und den black life matters protesten, die von Kamala Harris positiv betrachtet wurden. wo der ausloeser doch die ermordung von georg floyd und ein offensichtlicher bias von seiten der polizei herscht. die buergerrechts bewegung mit populistisch getriebenen und bewaffneten verschwoerungstheoretikern zu vergleichen ist reine provokation und populistic seiner seits. der rest seiner analyse jedoch ist wichtig und veranschaulicht den double standard sehr gut und die gefahren die von zu liberalem umgang mit bewegungen mit reinen eigen interesse und zerstoerrischen absichten (Monopole, Hegemonien, Totalitarismus) gegen pluralistische demokratische gesellschaften ausgehen.

Furthermore, I see a problem in Fergusons comparison, which is a general problem of US democracy, which is reinforcing a catholic binary world order. good or bad. any gradient in political analysis seems to really matter at the end of the day. the press in his view is polarised to the left, which he often claims, yet, the cases he presents should be evaluated under a more case specific lense. he is in fact populising himself, when talking about harris or biden in two totally different cases to proof his point. I argue that the examples he uses are not useful to argue his point. while mobilising to storm the parliament is an active attempt of a coup d'etat,  protest against police brutality that turn violent  (of course police brutality riots will enventually turn violent, we know that in germany, ACAB) is a not handled with enough respect for civil protest and disobedience. the latter one does not intend to rid a country of it's legal powers, but asks for acknoledgement of unequality and demands civil protection without bias.
the polical and economical relevanz is mixed in his arguments with ethical and humanitarian agendas. 

he does argue in another book that power is not only held by money alone, narrative and the control of the narrativ is, and we all know what sillicon valley will turn to once they see their actual chance to make more. if they can take out a government, they will. trump, thiel, besos and musk paved the way for them to fall. unfortunately for them until now, programmers liked leftist ideas, and they needed them. the CEOs that drove the goldrush only cared for themselfes, hence the exodus to mars ideas.

the last paragraph where he quotes orwell, and describes trump and musks agenda. which retrospetively is fantastic comedy seeing how these new alliances have formed.

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Residency Plan - 108.md

The aim is to produce the music for 108 versions of the themes of the songs of the album (W.T. "Preaching To The Choir"/ https://mandymozart.com/promo/preaching-to-the-choir/)  in a collaborative approach. 
Every collaboration is resulting in as many tracks as possible which can be released for audio visual TikTok loops.

108 stands for the 108 temptations one has to overcome on their way to Nirvana in Buddhism and stands for the bigger questions of why entities of many species and humans specifically engage in repetitions of rather complex procedures such as song and the very nature of us as a performative social creature as part of a greater digital world of content platforms. Specifically how submission to the algorithms content hunger may be seen as a potential for artistic liberation and creativity rather than a necessity to merely stay relevant.

Mandy Mozart embodies a pope-like figure who just recently found out about their own existence. That being a NPC in a open world game which was designed for cats. Knowing about their true nature triggers a plot of diverse quests in which the character tries hiding their fundamental discovery, differentiating reality from virtuality and exploring their new found super powers that came with the enlightenment. All in all, a playful phantasy which taps into everyday self-overestimation of male role models within our patriarchic society.

The residency is taking place at Westbahnstudios the entire April and June 2024.
Thatâ€™s two versions of a song recorded and live-streamed on Twitch & YouTube Live every day. One is recorded straight after arrival and one is recorded before leaving the studio. There is absolutely no style required. The music is the mood of the day. A necessity of prayer, a meditation, a ritual to overcome the temptations of the world. To reach a higher state of mind where bodies, minds and machines align and resonate. 
## Collaborations & Guests

Planned collaborations and streams as well as the recorded sessions will be exhibited online on a specific project website which functions as a hub to inform the audience, register and organise collaborators and archive the work in a comprehensive form.

Collaborators will be electronic musicians, singers (choir + soloists), brass and string instrument players, and audio visual artists and game developers.

During the day time we will be working on methodologies and sound with the invited artists.

A lava lamp, a sphynx cat sculpture and audio mobile are playing when no one is in the studio to deliver a 24/7 live stream in sort of a online Oracle which functions as a portal into the place of the content's creation.
The channel will be stopped twice every day and restarted to generate a daily routine and to overcome the 12h continuous streaming limit of the platforms.

A virtual and analog interconnected installation like a temple, a shrine, a digital spiritual town square with the announcements and subscriptions. Itâ€™s placed around the installation camera and tech.

**KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau e.V.**  
Hubertusweg 60  
13465 Berlin, Germany

**Date:** October 28, 2024

**To whom it may concern,**

This letter serves as proof of collaboration between KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau e.V. (KHF) and the invited artist, Tilman PorschÃ¼tz, for a planned residency and artistic project in Berlin, Germany.

**Invitation and Project Details**  
We are pleased to invite Mr. Tilman PorschÃ¼tz to participate in a collaborative residency at KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau from **February 17, 2025, to March 3, 2025**. During this residency, Mr. PorschÃ¼tz will be supported in his creative research, utilizing KHFâ€™s facilities and residency studios for the production of video art. Additionally, he will have the opportunity to share his work with the public during an open studio night, fostering dialogue and cultural exchange with the local community and other artists.

**About KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau (KHF)**  
Located in the scenic forested area of northern Berlin, KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau is a dynamic center for artistic production and discourse. Since its inception in 1998, KHF has provided over 4,000 square meters of studio space within a former hospital complex, welcoming painters, sculptors, ceramicists, writers, musicians, performers, and more. Our organization facilitates creative workspaces, awards the Dieter-Ruckhaberle-FÃ¶rderpreis, and organizes numerous artistic and cultural events supported by the Reinickendorf art council.





Kaya Behkalam  
Representative of KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Shorts\Grant Applications\Shorts - Mobility Grant.md

Description

Cat Pope is a poetic music and performance project about a god-like, cat-like creature trapped between digital and earthly realms. Inspired by spiritual influencers who share sermons, affirmations, and life advice to gain followers, I plan to produce around 70 short video art pieces that blend TikTok and Instagram content aesthetics. This fictional figure, a mix between a cat and a papal character, exists both digitally and physically. Collaborators include Korean special effects artist Una Ryu, Japanese videographer Hiroo Tanaka, and contributions from Patrizia Ruthensteiner (costumes), Tatjana StÃ¼rmer (graphics), Lukas Rehm (VFX), and more. The videos will be featured in 2025/26 through a dedicated social media account (goal: 25k followers in 3 months), an AR graphic novel (limited edition of 200), and physical installations at shows, exhibitions, art fairs, and film festivals across Europe.



Producing in Berlin allows me and Una Ryu to co-create the character Cat Pope, essential to the projectâ€™s artistic vision, with her special effects makeup as a cornerstone. The proximity to Ryuâ€™s workshop and a residency at KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau enable intensive, hands-on experimentation and collaboration, enhancing both creativity and efficiency by minimizing material transport costs and utilizing the seclusion of Frohnau for focused research. Working closely with award-winning videographer Hiroo Tanaka, known for his work with Atonal Festival and Ninja Tune, will expand our exploration of docu-fictional techniques, vital for the immersive nature of the project. The two-week Berlin residency is essential to achieve our objectives: creating a unique artistic work and exploring new conceptual approaches to blur digital and earthly realms through collaborative, concentrated development.

Main preparation steps for Cat Pope are underway: mask development is complete, with any alterations to be managed remotely. The costume is finalized, requiring no further work. A script for approximately 70 shorts is finished, with refinements ongoing with Hiroo Tanaka via digital correspondence. Weâ€™ve planned workshops on staging and scene design with Tanaka for pre-residency and the first week of residency. Filming will occur during the second week, followed by on-site and remote post-production. This structured preparation ensures a cohesive, efficient creative process.

The Cat Pope project aims to develop a distinctive visual and poetic language, establishing a foundation for the characterâ€™s future digital and analog performances, which will support further editions of video works, a graphic novel, and character evolution. This project will strengthen collaborations with our existing team, paving the way for sustained partnerships. In Berlin, I plan to network with galleries and exhibition spaces to promote a showcase and host an open studio day, connecting with the local art scene, curators, sponsors, and potential supporters. Additionally, I intend to initiate discussions on online promotion strategies to enhance the reach of this hybrid artwork. These steps are designed to expand both creative and professional opportunities.

To prioritize sustainability, the Berlin production is designed with eco-friendly actions. By relocating the production to Berlin, only my individual travelâ€”done by trainâ€”is required, reducing travel emissions. Local collaborations with Hiroo Tanaka and Una Ryu eliminate the need for long-distance shipping, as their studios are reachable via public transport. The KÃ¼nstlerhof residency provides on-site kitchen and accommodation, minimizing daily commuting and allowing us to source food locally. Additionally, we plan to re-use available materials at KÃ¼nstlerhof for props, reducing resource consumption, and will rent any necessary equipment locally, supporting sustainable practices throughout the project.

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Shorts\Prompts.md

Use when stuck in writing new stories.

You started a scam religion for a quick buck. You begin to panic when your fake god was actually a real forgotten one awakened from new worshippers, declared you it's high priest, and granted you the power of healing.

https://thinkwritten.com/365-creative-writing-prompts/

1.Â **Outside the Window**: Whatâ€™s the weather outside your window doing right now? If thatâ€™s not inspiring, whatâ€™s the weather like somewhere you wish you could be?

2.Â **The Unrequited love poem:**Â How do you feel when you love someone who does not love you back?

3.Â **The Vessel:**Â Write about a ship or other vehicle that can take you somewhere different from where you are now.

4.Â **Dancing:**Â Whoâ€™s dancing and why are they tapping those toes?

5.Â **Food:**Â Whatâ€™s for breakfast? Dinner? Lunch? Or maybe you could write a poem about that time you met a friend at a cafe.

6.Â **Eye Contact:**Â Write about two people seeing each other for the first time.

7.Â **The Rocket-ship:**Â Write about a rocket-ship on its way to the moon or a distant galaxy far, far, away.

8.Â **Dream-catcher**: Write somethingÂ inspired by a recent dream you had.

9.Â **Animals:**Â Choose an animal. Write about it!

10.Â **Friendship:**Â Write about being friends with someone.

11.Â **Dragon**: Envision a dragon. Do you battle him? Or is the dragon friendly? Use descriptive language.

12.Â **Greeting**: Write a story or poem that starts with the word â€œhelloâ€ or another greeting.

13.Â **The Letter:**Â Write a poem or story using words from a famous letter or inspired by a letter someone sent you.

## Objective
Based on Cat Pope Character the aim is to produce a collection of approx. 70 social media shorts and a series of cat and cucumber videos. FYI, I collected a list of inspirations in this list: https://github.com/mandymozart/memexprime/blob/main/Projects/Pocket%20Preacher/Shorts/Shorts%20-%20Research%20and%20inspirations%20(to%20reenact).md
### Duration 
approx. 2-3 days shooting during 17.2. - 3.3.2025
Additional meetings for shoot planning and stage setup may be necessary. 
## Location
*  streamer corner, have cave, have a cat tree
* Small Indoor studio available at KÃ¼nstlerhof Frohnau, Berlin
* Bathroom
* Overnight accommodations possible, private rooms, kitchen, etc.
* public transport approx. 45 minutes from Berlin main station
## Requirements
### SFX Makeup
- Re-use of the Cat Pope mask (for convenience)
* Application and maintenance of makeup during shoots
### Video
* Orientation: Portrait
* dynamic multi-cam setup imitating podcaster vibe
* Studio Lighting (Some rollei Lights avaiable in Vienna)
* Teleprompter (I got one here in Vienna, but it is tricky to use, with the shitty ipad app)
### Stage Design/Scenography
* Blogger/Podcaster Studio setup on sight in the indoor studio (first week)
* stage a exhibit able cat tree an angel a cat neon tube of the logo, bootleg Dagobert, a line art cat pope illustration , 
* Some of the stainless windows (5 stages of grief which is the outline of awakening) scenes 
* Potential Outdoor locations if applicable 
### Script
* I will have all shorts scripted out before the start of the residency 
* Script will follow a standard screenplay format and can be prompted as instructions via the app.
* Exhibition > you will get a prompt via the app inside the studio staging and can record an interpretation

## File: Projects\Pocket Preacher\Shorts\Shorts - Import Log, Format and Conventions.md

# Purpose of this file 

Streamline the note keeping for shorts to fit a standardised format. Ultimately this should make import automation into the repository easier. 
## Import Log

Each line is an import with date and a short description of what was imported. Consider it a commit to the NLP source data repository of the cat pope script.  

Import: 2024-11-28 Import_message: initial Import 

## Format & Convention 

Add new short discoveries to the top of the file.

All entries should be a single line. 

Each note should start with a short scene description, introducing the character and pov. Followed by the main dialog transcription. You can already replace characters with cat pope or relevant alternative characters who could also Playout this scene. Example: Priest/Butcher/CEO 

Continue with hashtags, both from the original short and your own. 

Copy and paste the url or image after that. 

Add additional notes after that. Most common choices are Caption or Reenactment instructions and remarks on how to mutate the source.

### Example 

INT. HOTEL CORRIDOR An elegantly dressed Lady/Pope approaches POV SCEPTIC. SCEPTIC (O.S.) Hey you, you look great today. LADY/POPE (shy) Thank you. You too. {FART} #comedy #pickupartist #sin  https://instagram.com/somehashid Caption: This is how you will succeed every time â€¦ Remark: should change the fart to offering a cucumber and leave in rush giggling.
